================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Hardtop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Hardtop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Hardtop_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Hardtop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Hardtop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Hardtop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Hardtop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Hardtop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Hardtop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Hardtop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Explorer → CSC Slicktop Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Explorer/CSC_Slicktop_Explorer/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/Transport_Vehicles/CSC_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → Transport Vehicles → CSC F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/Transport_Vehicles/CSC_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → Transport Vehicles → CSC F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/Transport_Vehicles/CSC_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → Transport Vehicles → CSC F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
			v.Light.Enabled = true
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
			v.Light.Enabled = false
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/Transport_Vehicles/CSC_F-350/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → Transport Vehicles → CSC F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/Transport_Vehicles/CSC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → Transport Vehicles → CSC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/Transport_Vehicles/CSC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → Transport Vehicles → CSC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/Transport_Vehicles/CSC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → Transport Vehicles → CSC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights2;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/Transport_Vehicles/CSC_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → Transport Vehicles → CSC Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.G1)
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.G2)
	
	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2) 
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					G1(1);
					G2(1);	
					wait()			
				end
			end)
		end)()		


		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					R5(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R6(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));						
					wait(0.15)						

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		

					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		
				end
			end)
		end)()		
				
		
	else
		G1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
		G2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));						
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)		
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local centre = brakelights.Centre;
	local top = brakelights.Top;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
		brakelights.Top.Material = smoothMaterial;
		brakelights.Top.Light.Enabled = false;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_14_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
local headlightState = script.Parent.Parent.State.Headlights;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = true;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = false;
			wait(0.5);
		end; 
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = (headlightState.Value == true and neonMaterial or smoothMaterial);
		indicatorRear.Light.Enabled = headlightState.Value;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_14_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT '14 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT Explorer → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)

	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2) 
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);		
				wait()	
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					R5(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R6(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));						
					wait(0.15)						

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		

					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		
				end
			end)
		end)()		
				
		
	else
		T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
		T5(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));						
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)		
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
	end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_Explorer/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern2.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern2 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT Explorer → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)

	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2) 
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
				F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
				F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));

					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);

				end
			end)
		end)()		
				
		
	else
		T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));						
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)		
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_Explorer/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	--Front Lightbar lights
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1)
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2)
	local T3 = elsModule(ELSModel.T3)
	local T4 = elsModule(ELSModel.T4)
	local T5 = elsModule(ELSModel.T5)
	local T6 = elsModule(ELSModel.T6)
	local T7 = elsModule(ELSModel.T7)
	local T8 = elsModule(ELSModel.T8)

	--Front lights
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1)
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2)
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3)
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4)

	--Back lights lights
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1)
	local R2 = elsModule(ELSModel.R2) 
	local R3 = elsModule(ELSModel.R3)
	local R4 = elsModule(ELSModel.R4)
	local R5 = elsModule(ELSModel.R5)
	local R6 = elsModule(ELSModel.R6)
	local R7 = elsModule(ELSModel.R7)
	local R8 = elsModule(ELSModel.R8)

	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait()						
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);		
				wait()	
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R2(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					R5(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R6(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R7(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));
					R8(1, Color3.fromRGB(82, 124, 174));						
					wait(0.15)						

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		

					R1(0);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(0);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);

					wait(0.02)

					R2(1);

					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.15)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);

				wait(0.15)					
					
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait(0.12)						
						
				F1(1);	
				F2(0);	
				F3(0);	
				F4(1);					
				wait(0.15)						
					
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait(0.12)						
						
				F1(1);	
				F2(0);	
				F3(0);	
				F4(1);					
				wait(0.15)						
					
				F1(1);	
				F2(1);	
				F3(1);	
				F4(1);					
				wait(0.12)							
					
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				T5(1);
				T6(1);
				T7(1);
				T8(1);		
				wait()	
				end
			end)
		end)()		

		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					R1(0 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		

					R1(0);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(0);
					R5(1);
					R6(0);
					R7(0);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.12)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.12)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)			

					R1(1);
					R2(0);
					R3(0);
					R4(1);
					R5(0);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(0);			
					wait(0.12)		

					R1(1);
					R2(1);
					R3(1);
					R4(1);
					R5(1);
					R6(1);
					R7(1);
					R8(1);			
					wait(0.02)		
					
				end
			end)
		end)()		
				
		
	else
		T1(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T2(1 ,Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
		T4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
		T5(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T6(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T7(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
		T8(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));						
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		R3(1)
		R4(1)
		R5(1)
		R6(1)
		R7(1)
		R8(1)		
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSC_ERT/CSC_ERT_F-350/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSC:ERT → CSC:ERT F-350 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSOR/CSOR/CSOR_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSOR → CSOR → CSOR G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;

	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSOR/CSOR/CSOR_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSOR → CSOR → CSOR G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for _,v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		end
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSOR/CSOR/CSOR_G-Wagon/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSOR → CSOR → CSOR G-Wagon → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSOR/CSOR/CSOR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSOR → CSOR → CSOR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSOR/CSOR/CSOR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSOR → CSOR → CSOR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSOR/CSOR/CSOR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSOR → CSOR → CSOR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSOR/CSOR/CSOR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSOR → CSOR → CSOR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/CSOR/CSOR/CSOR_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → CSOR → CSOR → CSOR Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:40
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local B5 = elsModule(ELSModel.B5);
	local B6 = elsModule(ELSModel.B6);
	local B7 = elsModule(ELSModel.B7);
	local B8 = elsModule(ELSModel.B8);
	local LS1 = elsModule(ELSModel.LS1);
	local LS2 = elsModule(ELSModel.LS2);
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1);
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2);
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3);
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4);
	local RS1 = elsModule(ELSModel.RS1);
	local RS2 = elsModule(ELSModel.RS2);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local F8 = elsModule(ELSModel.F8);
	local K1 = elsModule(ELSModel.K1);
	local K2 = elsModule(ELSModel.K2);

	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					B5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					B6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					B7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

					LS2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Department_of_Business_Affairs/DoBA_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Department of Business Affairs → DoBA Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Department_of_Business_Affairs/DoBA_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Department of Business Affairs → DoBA Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Department_of_Business_Affairs/DoBA_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Department of Business Affairs → DoBA Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Department_of_Business_Affairs/DoBA_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Department of Business Affairs → DoBA Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_Diplomat/FS_Diplomat_Tahoe/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone Diplomat → FS Diplomat Tahoe → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local elsModule = script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)

	--front lights
	local F1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F2);

	local R1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R1);
	local R2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R2);	

	if enabled then
		F1(0)
		F2(0)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
	else
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)		
	end
end

--[[

    Parent: FSP:ESU Explorer

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Explorer/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Explorer → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local elsModule = script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)

	--front lights
	local D1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.D1);
	local D2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.D2);

	local F1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F2);

	local R1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R1);
	local R2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.R2);

	--rear & amber visor lights
	local AL = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.AL);
	local AR = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.AR);

	if enabled then
		F1(0)
		F2(0)
		D1(0)
		D2(0)
		R1(0)
		R2(0)
		AL(0)
		AR(0)
	else
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		D1(1)
		D2(1)
		R1(1)
		R2(1)
		AL(1)
		AR(1)
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SurfaceGui') then
			part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SurfaceGui').Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
		end;
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Flag_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Flag Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Flag_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Flag Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Firestone_State_Patrol_ESU/FSP_ESU_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Firestone State Patrol: ESU → FSP:ESU Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

game:GetService('ServerScriptService'):WaitForChild('AeroLoaded');

local Colours = {
	Color3.fromRGB(56, 58, 56),
	Color3.fromRGB(105, 102, 92),
	Color3.fromRGB(80, 109, 84),
	Color3.fromRGB(150, 85, 85),
	Color3.fromRGB(213, 115, 61),
	Color3.fromRGB(136, 62, 62),
	Color3.fromRGB(90, 76, 66),
	Color3.fromRGB(105, 102, 92),
	Color3.fromRGB(27, 42, 53),
	Color3.fromRGB(40, 127, 71)
}

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, true);

local randomColor = math.random(1,#Colours)
_G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService:PaintCar(script.Parent, Colours[randomColor])


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Charger/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Charger → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local X1 = elsModule(ELSModel.X1);
	local X2 = elsModule(ELSModel.X2);
	local X3 = elsModule(ELSModel.X3);
	local X4 = elsModule(ELSModel.X4);
	local R1 = elsModule(ELSModel.R1);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					X1(0);
					X2(1);
					X3(0);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.04)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					X3(1);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.04)
					X1(0);
					X2(1);
					X3(0);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.04)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					X3(1);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.04)
					X1(1);
					X2(0);
					X3(1);
					X4(0);
					wait(0.04)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					X3(1);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.04)
					X1(1);
					X2(0);
					X3(1);
					X4(0);
					wait(0.04)
					X1(1);
					X2(1);
					X3(1);
					X4(1);
					wait(0.04)
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					R1(0);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(1);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(0);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(1);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(0);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(1);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(0);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(1);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(0);
					wait(0.08)
					R1(1);
					wait(0.5)
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		X1(1);
		X2(1);	
		X3(1);
		X4(1);	
		R1(1);	
	end
end

    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;

				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

	return _G.Aero.Shared.INSETest(plr);
end;
