================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Durango/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.BrakeLights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Durango/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Durango/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.BrakeLights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Durango/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Durango → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

]]

	-18,
	0,
	26,
	46,
	61,
	76,
	101,
	121
};


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

local Colours = {
	Color3.fromRGB(56, 58, 56),
	Color3.fromRGB(105, 102, 92),

	Color3.fromRGB(150, 85, 85),

	Color3.fromRGB(27, 42, 53),
	Color3.fromRGB(40, 127, 71)
}

_G.Aero.Modules.Car.new(script.Parent, true);

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Sprinter/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Sprinter → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local elsModule = script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart;

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local T1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T2);
	local T3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T3);
	local T4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.T4);
	if enabled then
		task.defer(pcall, function()
			while true do
				T1(0);
				T2(1);
				T3(0);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)					

				T1(0);
				T2(1);
				T3(0);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)	

				T1(1);
				T2(0);
				T3(1);
				T4(0);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)						

				T1(1);
				T2(0);
				T3(1);
				T4(0);
				wait(0.09)

				T1(1);
				T2(1);
				T3(1);
				T4(1);
				wait(0.02)									
			end
		end)

	else
		T1(1)
		T2(1)
		T3(1)
		T4(1)
	end
end

		T4(1)
	end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Sprinter/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Sprinter → Config → Modules

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = neonMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;

			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		body.Headlights.Logo.Material = smoothMaterial
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/GCPS_INSET-ERT/Ops_Sprinter/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → GCPS (INSET-ERT) → Ops Sprinter → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;
	local reverseSound = body.Parent.Chassis.Platform.Sounds.Reverse

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			reverseSound:Play();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			reverseSound:Stop();
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Cadet/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Cadet → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);

			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Cadet/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Cadet → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Cadet/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Cadet → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.RotLights.F1.Light);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.RotLights.F2.Light);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.RotLights.F3.Light);
	local M1 = elsModule(ELSModel.RotLights.M1.Light);
	local G1 = elsModule(ELSModel.RotLights.G1.Light);
	local G2 = elsModule(ELSModel.RotLights.G2.Light);
	local G3 = elsModule(ELSModel.RotLights.G3.Light);
	local D1 = elsModule(ELSModel.D1);
	local D2 = elsModule(ELSModel.D2);	
	local E1 = elsModule(ELSModel.E1);
	local E2 = elsModule(ELSModel.E2);
	local E3 = elsModule(ELSModel.E3);
	local E4 = elsModule(ELSModel.E4);	
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F3(0);
					F2(0);
					F1(0);
					M1(0);					
					G1(0);
					G2(0);
					G3(0);	
					D1(0);
					D2(0);
					E1(0);
					E2(0);	
					E3(0);
					E4(0);	
					wait();
				end
			end)
		end)

	else
		F3(1);
		F2(1);
		F1(1);
		M1(1);					
		G1(1);
		G2(1);
		G3(1);	
		F3(1);
		F2(1);
		F1(1);
		M1(1);					
		G1(1);
		G2(1);
		G3(1);	
		D1(1);
		D2(1);
		E1(1);
		E2(1);	
		E3(1);
		E4(1);	
	end;
end;

					E4(1);		
					wait(.09);						
				end
			end)
		end)				
		
		while true do
			for i = 1, 360, 15 do
				for i2, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
					local orientation = Vector3.new(0, v.OppositeDirection.Value and -i or i, 0);
					v.Chrome.Orientation = orientation;
					v.Light.Orientation = orientation;
				end;
				wait();
			end;
			wait();
		end;
	else
		H1(1);
		H2(1);
		D1(1);
		D2(1);
		E1(1);
		E2(1);	
		E3(1);
		E4(1);	
		for i, v in next, ELSModel.RotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = false;
			v.Light.Transparency = 1;	
		end;
	end;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Dodge_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Dodge Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Dodge_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Dodge Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Dodge_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Dodge Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Dodge_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Dodge Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/NSEC/NSEC_Dodge_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC Dodge Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

    Pattern2 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → NSEC → NSEC F-150 → Body → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:43
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart)

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local L1 = elsModule(ELSModel.L1);
	local L2 = elsModule(ELSModel.L2);
	local L3 = elsModule(ELSModel.L3);
	local L4 = elsModule(ELSModel.L4);
	local L5 = elsModule(ELSModel.L5);
	local L6 = elsModule(ELSModel.L6);
	local L7 = elsModule(ELSModel.L7);
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local M1 = elsModule(ELSModel.M1);
	local M2 = elsModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = elsModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = elsModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = elsModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = elsModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = elsModule(ELSModel.M7);
	local M8 = elsModule(ELSModel.M8);


	if enabled then
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));					
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));				
					L1(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					L2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					L3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					L4(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));				
					wait(0.03)

					F1(0);
					F2(0);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)

					F1(1);
					F2(0);
					F3(0);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)					

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(0);
					F4(0);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)					

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(0);
					L1(0);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)	

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(0);
					L2(0);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)	

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(0);
					L3(0);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)						

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(0);
					L4(0);
					wait(0.03)											

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(0);
					L3(0);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)							

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(0);
					L2(0);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)							

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(0);
					L1(0);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)	

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(0);
					F4(0);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)	

					F1(1);
					F2(0);
					F3(0);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)	

					F1(0);
					F2(0);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)						

					F1(0);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)						

					F1(1);
					F2(1);
					F3(1);
					F4(1);
					L1(1);
					L2(1);
					L3(1);
					L4(1);
					wait(0.03)		
					
				end
			end)
		end)()
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do	
					F5(0);
					F6(0);
					F7(0);
					L5(0);
					L6(0);
					L7(0);				
					wait(0.13)	

					F5(1);
					F6(1);
					F7(1);
					L5(1);
					L6(1);
					L7(1);				
					wait(0.08)	
				end
			end)
		end)()

		
		
		coroutine.wrap(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do	
					M1(0, Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0));
					M2(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));		
					M3(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					M4(1, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));				
					M5(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					M6(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					M7(0, Color3.fromRGB(218, 133, 65));
					M8(1, Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 0));			
					wait(0.15)

					M1(1);
					M2(1);	
					M3(1);
					M4(1);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(1);
					M8(1);					
					wait(0.085)	

					M1(0);
					M2(1);	
					M3(1);
					M4(1);
					M5(0);
					M6(0);
					M7(0);
					M8(1);					
					wait(0.15)	

					M1(1);
					M2(1);	
					M3(1);
					M4(1);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(1);
					M8(1);					
					wait(0.085)	

					M1(1);
					M2(0);	
					M3(0);
					M4(0);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(1);
					M8(0);					
					wait(0.15)	

					M1(1);
					M2(1);	
					M3(1);
					M4(1);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(1);
					M8(1);					
					wait(0.085)	

					M1(1);
					M2(0);	
					M3(0);
					M4(0);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(1);
					M8(0);					
					wait(0.15)	

					M1(1);
					M2(1);	
					M3(1);
					M4(1);
					M5(1);
					M6(1);
					M7(1);
					M8(1);					
					wait(0.085)	
				end
			end)
		end)()

	else
		L1(1);
		L2(1);
		L3(1);
		L4(1);
		L5(1);
		L6(1);
		L7(1);
		F1(1);
		F2(1);
		F3(1);
		F4(1);
		F5(1);
		F6(1);
		F7(1);		
		M1(1);
		M2(1);
		M3(1);
		M4(1);
		M5(1);
		M6(1);
		M7(1);
		M8(1);
		M7(1);
		M8(1);		
	end
end

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local L1 = elsModule(ELSModel.L1);
